## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (rate laws / concentration-time ODE models)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is explicitly the time-derivative of a reactant concentration A, which is the standard object modeled by chemical kinetics rate laws. With only (t, A) available, the most likely structures are autonomous or time-modulated kinetic ODEs where dA_dt depends on A (reaction order, reversibility, autocatalysis) and possibly explicit time dependence via changing conditions or catalyst activity.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order consumption: dA_dt = -c0 (constant-rate depletion when surface/photochemical rate-limited)
- First-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay or pseudo-first-order conditions)
- Second-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular 2A -> products, or effective second order)
- General n-th order law: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical overall order / lumped kinetics)
- Mixed-order (1st + 2nd): dA_dt = -c0 * A - c1 * A**2 (parallel pathways with different orders)
- Equilibrium relaxation (linear driving force): dA_dt = -c0 * (A - c1) (approach to steady/equilibrium concentration c1)
- Reversible first-order (A ↔ B with B eliminated via A+B=c2): dA_dt = -c0 * A + c1 * (c2 - A) (net rate from forward/back reactions under conservation)
- Autocatalytic / logistic-type kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-accelerating then self-limiting dynamics)
- Autoinhibition / crowding rational rate: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (1 + c1 * A) (rate slows at high A due to inhibition/limited capacity)
- Time-ramped first-order rate constant: dA_dt = -(c0 + c1 * t) * A (changing conditions causing k(t) to drift linearly)
- Catalyst deactivation / fading activity: dA_dt = -c0 * exp(-c1 * t) * A (effective k(t) decays with time)
- Periodic forcing (e.g., light modulation): dA_dt = -c0 * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * A (time-periodic rate coefficient)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- If dA_dt depends only on A (no explicit t), the system is likely time-invariant kinetics; scatter of dA_dt vs A collapses onto a single curve.
- Linear relation dA_dt ∝ -A indicates first-order behavior; log(A) vs t tends toward a straight line in the implied solution.
- Strong curvature with dA_dt magnitude increasing faster than linearly in A suggests higher-order (A**c1 with c1>1) or additional A**2 term.
- A nonzero intercept in dA_dt vs A near A≈0 suggests zero-order contributions (mass-transfer/surface-limited steps).
- Sign change of dA_dt around A≈c1 indicates relaxation toward an equilibrium/steady concentration (driving-force form -(A-c1)).
- Initial acceleration (dA_dt increasing with A at low A) plus later slowdown near a ceiling suggests autocatalysis with a limiting term A*(c1-A).
- Explicit time dependence (e.g., drift in dA_dt at fixed A) points to k(t) modulation such as deactivation exp(-c*t), ramp (c0+c1*t), or periodic sin(c*t).
- A rational inhibitory form A/(1+c*A) is suggested when rate increases with A at low A but becomes approximately constant (or less sensitive) at high A.

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK14)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A*exp(-c2*_s*t) + c3*_p*sin(c4*A)
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed function):
\[
f(t,A)= -k\sqrt{A}\;-\;k\,A\,e^{-\lambda t}\;+\;B\sin(\omega A)
\]
with \(k=0.1286242133\), \(\lambda=0.0593843782\), \(B=0.3894244877\), \(\omega=0.5829315814\).
Key structural facts:
- Has an unavoidable \(\sqrt{A}\) term (nonlinear in \(A\), no \(t\)-dependence).
- Has an \(A\cdot e^{-\lambda t}\) term (product of \(A\) and an exponential in \(t\)).
- Has a \(\sin(\omega A)\) term with **no phase shift** and **no \(t\)**.
- No rational-in-\(t\) terms like \(1/(t+c)\), no \(\log\), no \(\tanh\), etc.

Now check candidates for whether any parameter choice can reproduce exactly those three components and nothing else.

1. \(A c0 + A c1/(c2+t)+ c3\sin(Ac4+c5)+ c6 e^{c7 t}+ c8/(c2+c9 t)\)  
   Only linear-in-\(A\) and rational-in-\(t\) pieces; no \(\sqrt{A}\). Also exponential term is not multiplied by \(A\). Cannot match.

2. \(A c0 + A c1/(c2 t+c3)+ c4\sin(Ac5+c6)+ c7 e^{c8 t}+ c9/(c3+t)\)  
   Same issues: no \(\sqrt{A}\); exponential not multiplied by \(A\); extra rational terms. Cannot.

3. \(A c0/(c1+t)+ c2+ c3\sin(Ac4+c5)+ c6 e^{c7 t}+ c8/(c1+c9 t)\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Also \(A\) only appears as \(A/(t+\cdot)\) and in sine; cannot create \(-k\sqrt{A}\) nor \(A e^{-\lambda t}\). Cannot.

4. \(A c0/(c1+t)+ c2+ c3\sin(\cdot)+ c6 e^{c7 t}+ c8 t + t\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\); wrong \(t\)-polynomial terms. Cannot.

5. Same as 4 with more \(t\) terms. Cannot.

6. \(A c0/(c1+t)+ c2 t + c3 + c4\sin(\cdot)+ c7 e^{c8 t)\)}  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\); exponential not multiplied by \(A\). Cannot.

7. \(A c0/(c1+t)+ c2 + c3 t + c4\sin(\cdot)+ c7 e^{c8 t)+ c9 t}\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

8. \(A c0/(c1 t+c2)+ c3 + c4\sin(\cdot)+ c7 e^{c8 t}+ c9/(c2+t)\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\); has rational terms. Cannot.

9. \(A c0/(c1 t+c2)+ c3 + c4\sin(\cdot)+ c7 e^{c8 t}+ c9/(c1 t+c2)\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

10. \(A c0/(c1 t+c2)+ c3\sin(\cdot)+ c6 e^{c7 t}+ c8/(c2+t)\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\); exponential not multiplied by \(A\). Cannot.

11. \(A c0/(c1+t)+ c2\sin(\cdot)+ c5 e^{c6 t}+ c7/(c1+c8 t)\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

12. Includes \((c2+t)^{-1/3}\) and \(\tanh\); no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

13. \(A c0 + A c1/(c2+t)+ c3\sin(\cdot)+ c6 e^{c7 t}+ c8/(c2+t)\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\); also exponential not multiplied by \(A\). Cannot.

14. Similar: no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

15. Has \(A(c1+t)^{c2}\), \(\log(Ac4+1)\), etc.; no \(\sqrt{A}\) term and wrong \(t\)-dependence. Cannot.

16. \(A c0/\sqrt{c1+t} + c2\sin(c3 t+c4)+ c5\sin(Ac6+c7)+ c8 e^{c9 t}\)  
   Still no \(\sqrt{A}\) (it’s \(A/\sqrt{t+\cdot}\)). Also introduces \(\sin\) in \(t\). Cannot.

17. \(A c0/(c1 t+c2)+ A c3 + c4 + c5\sin(\cdot)+ c8 e^{c9 t}+ 1/(c1 t+c2)\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\); exponential not multiplied by \(A\). Cannot.

18. Similar: no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

19. Has \(\log(c5 t+1)\) and \(t(A+c7)^{c8}\); no \(\sqrt{A}\) standalone. Cannot.

20. \(A c0 + A c1/(c2+t)+ c3\sin(\cdot)+ c6 e^{c7 t}+ c8\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\); exponential not multiplied by \(A\). Cannot.

21. Similar: no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

22. \(A c0/\sqrt{c1+t} + c2\sin(Ac3+c4)+ c5\sin(Ac6+c7)+ c8 e^{c9 t}\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\); also has two sine-in-\(A\) terms but still cannot generate \(-k\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

23. Has \(\log\) and \(\exp(Ac4)\); no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

24. \(A c0/(c1+t)+ c2 t + c3 + c4\sin(\cdot)+ c7/(c1+c8 t)\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

25. \(A c0/(c1 t+c2)+ c3 t + c4 + c5\sin(\cdot)+ c8/(c2+t)\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

26. \(A c0/\sqrt{c1+t} + A^{c2}c3 + c4\sin(\cdot)+ c7 e^{c8 t}+ c9\)  
   Has an \(A^{c2}\) term, so one might try \(c2=\tfrac12\) to get \(\sqrt{A}\). But then it produces \(c3\sqrt{A}\) **and** also has \(A/\sqrt{t+\cdot}\) and an exponential term not multiplied by \(A\). You can zero out \(A/\sqrt{t+\cdot}\) by \(c0=0\) and zero out constant \(c9=0\), but you still cannot form \(-k A e^{-\lambda t}\) because the exponential term is \(c7 e^{c8 t}\) with no \(A\) factor, and the remaining \(A^{c2}\) term has no \(t\). Cannot.

27. \(A c0/\sqrt{c1+t} + c2\sin(Ac3+c4)+ c5 e^{A c6}+ c7 e^{c8 t}+ c9\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\) term; also has \(e^{A c6}\). Cannot.

28. Similar with \(\log(Ac6+1)\); no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

29. \(A c0/\sqrt{c1+t} + A c2 + c3 + c4\sin(\cdot)+ c7 e^{c8 t}\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

30. \(A c0/(c1+t)+ c2 t + c3\sin(\cdot)+ c6 e^{c7 t}\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\); exponential not multiplied by \(A\). Cannot.

31. \(A c0/(c1+t)+ c2\sin(\cdot)+ c5 e^{c6 t}+ c7 t + t\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

32. Similar: no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

33. \(A c0(c1+t)^{c2}+ c3+ c4\sin(\cdot)+ c7 e^{c8 t}\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

34. Similar rational mix: no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

35. \(A c0/\sqrt{c1+t}+ c2\sin(\cdot)+ c5\log(Ac6+1)+ c7 e^{c8 t}\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

36. Has \(\exp(Ac4)\) and logs; no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

38. Similar: no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

40. Everything divided by \((c1 t+c2)\); no \(\sqrt{A}\) and wrong structure. Cannot.

41. Same as 40. Cannot.

42. \(A c0/\sqrt{c1+t} + A c2 (c3+t)^{c4}+ c5\sin(\cdot)+ c8 e^{c9 t}\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Also cannot produce \(A e^{-\lambda t}\) because exponential term lacks \(A\) factor, and the \(A\)-dependent \(t\)-factor is a power, not exponential. Cannot.

43. Has \(\sin(c5 t+c6)\) and \(\log(c2 e^{A c3}+1)\); no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

45. Has \((c2+t)^{-1/3}\) and \(\tanh\); no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

46. Has \(A(c1+t)^{c2}\) and \(t^{c4}\); no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

47. \(A c0(c1+t)^{c2} + A + c3\sin(\cdot)+ c6 e^{c7 t}\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\); also has unavoidable \(+A\) unless set by parameter? (It’s literal \(A\), cannot be removed). Cannot.

48. \(A c0 + A(c1+t)^{c2}+ c3\sin(\cdot)+ c6 e^{c7 t}\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

49. \(A c0 + A c1 (c2+t)^{c3}+ c4\sin(\cdot)+ c7 e^{c8 t}\)  
   No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

50. Has \(\tanh\) and \(t/(c9+t)\); no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot.

Conclusion: none of the candidates can generate the required standalone \(-k\sqrt{A}\) term **and** the required \(-k A e^{-\lambda t}\) coupling simultaneously (most have neither \(\sqrt{A}\) nor an \(A\)-scaled exponential in \(t\)).

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK14)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A*exp(-c2*_s*t) + c3*_p*sin(c4*A)
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.1286*sqrt(A) - 0.1286*A*exp(-0.0594*t) + 0.3894*sin(0.5829*A)`

The GT has three terms:
1. `-c0*sqrt(A)` — a sqrt(A) term
2. `-c1*A*exp(-c2*_s*t)` — an A·exp(decay·t) term
3. `c3*_p*sin(c4*A)` — a sin(A) term (no phase shift, pure sin of scaled A)

Key basis functions in GT: `sqrt(A)`, `A*exp(αt)`, `sin(βA)`

Now let me analyze each candidate. The candidates generally have structures like:
- `A/(c+t)` or `A/sqrt(c+t)` or `A*(c+t)^p` — rational/power functions of t times A
- `sin(A*c + c)` — sinusoidal in A
- `exp(c*t)` — exponential in t
- Various additional terms

**Critical observation:** The GT has `A*exp(-αt)` which is NOT the same as `A/(c+t)` or `A/sqrt(c+t)` or `A*(c+t)^c` for any constant choices. These are fundamentally different functions of t. An exponential decay cannot equal a rational function or power function of t for all t.

However, `A*(c1+t)^c2` with `c2` free CAN'T match `A*exp(αt)` because power functions and exponentials are linearly independent.

Similarly, `A/(c+t)` = `A*(c+t)^(-1)` is a power function, not an exponential.

Let me check if any candidate has BOTH `A*exp(ct)` AND `sqrt(A)` terms:

Looking through all candidates, I need to find ones with:
1. A `sqrt(A)` term (or `A^(1/2)`)
2. An `A*exp(ct)` term
3. A `sin(cA)` term

**None of the candidates have an explicit `sqrt(A)` term.** 

But wait - some candidates have `A^c` terms or `log(A+1)` terms. Let me check:

- **Candidate 26:** `A*c0/sqrt(c1+t) + A^c2*c3 + c4*sin(...) + c7*exp(c8*t) + c9` — Has `A^c2` which could be `sqrt(A)` if c2=0.5. But it lacks `A*exp(ct)`. The `A/sqrt(c1+t)` term is not `A*exp(ct)`.

- **Candidate 33:** `A*c0*(c1+t)^c2 + c3 + c4*sin(...) + c7*exp(c8*t)` — `A*(c1+t)^c2` cannot equal `A*exp(αt)` for all t.

- **Candidate 15:** `A*c0*(c1+t)^c2 + c3*log(A*c4+1) + c5*sin(...) + c8*exp(c9*t)` — Same issue.

- **Candidate 49:** `A*c0 + A*c1*(c2+t)^c3 + c4*sin(...) + c7*exp(c8*t)` — `A*(c2+t)^c3` ≠ `A*exp(αt)`.

No candidate simultaneously has `sqrt(A)`, `A*exp(ct)`, and `sin(cA)`. The GT requires these three specific basis functions, and none of the candidates provide all three.

Going through all 50 candidates systematically: None have both a `sqrt(A)` (or equivalent `A^0.5`) term AND an `A*exp(ct)` term. The exponential terms in candidates are always standalone `exp(ct)`, never multiplied by A. And no candidate has a pure `sqrt(A)` basis function.
